data-tag="RelatedQnA.ItemDetails"><div><div class="rwrl rwrl_small rwrl_padref">Settlement is the delivery of securities to complete trades. It involves upgrading personal rights into property rights and thus protects market participants from the risk of the default of their counterparties. Immobilisation and dematerialisation are the two broad goals of electronic settlement.</div><div class="rwrl_cred rwrl_f"><div class="qna_algo"><div class="b_algo"><p><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Settlement_(finance)" h="ID=SERP,6369.1">Settlement (finance) - Wikipedia</a></p></div><div class="b_attribution b_clearfix "><cite>en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Settlement_(finance)</cite></div></div></div></div><div class="df_rq rwrl_small"><strong>Search for: </strong><a href="/search?q=What%20is%20electronic%20settlement%20in%20trading%3F" h="ID=SERP,6370.1">What is electronic settlement in trading?</a></div></div></div></div></div><div class="df_topAlAs df_sideColor df_alsoAsk df_close " data-tag="RelatedQnA.Item" data-query="What is settlement in trading?" data-IID="SERP.6371" data-ParentIID="SERP.6372"><div class="b_module_expansion_control b_module_head"><div class="b_module_expansion"><div class="b_expansion_wrapper b_expand b_divsec  b_onpage_expansion " data-wire="I;expei;;
